<gmapID>0x54d15744c6ac11fb:0x457ec5794edf3771<//gmapID>< text>
Fun for toddlers to older kids because it has a wide variety of fun climbing and spinning structures. We usually spend about 2 hours here! Kids should wear good climbing shoes. IMPORTANT: No bathrooms at this park!! There is a picnic table and a nice sidewalk surrounding the play area, so kids like to bring scooters to go around and around. There is also a nice large grassy lawn, but it seems rarely mowed, so it is often very wet.<//text>

< text>
This place is amazing! My daughter's Iphone had salt water damage. In the interim she somehow managed to get her Iphone 5s working, which by the way, had a badly damaged screen. We had initially taken the phone to the place she previously had her phone screen fixed. Really nice guys, but in this case, he stated that he would have to send it out to a third party and had no confidence that it would be fixed. He had suggested that we buy a new phone. I am stubborn, so I had my daughter look for places around the area and she found CIR. I was greeted by Eddie, older guy of the two.  I told him about the salt water damage, Eddie explained that salt causes other internal corrosion. He quickly did a motherboard test and gave us some hope, but even though he might be able to fix it, the salt might continue to do damage. He suggested with any water damage especially salt it's important to bring it in quickly as he has a solution he is able to dip it in. After he explained those risks, we decided to give it a go. Thuc tested all the functions of the phone cleaned the outside and had already place a free screen protector! Reasonable and fast, I would highly recommend this place! Definitely my location to get my tech items fixed.
